  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1e4f2975-dc11-4059-b161-1fd245729cce'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText53094639446797702" style="display:none">The seventh and final book in the #1 New York Times bestselling I Am Number Four series! With United as One, this action-packed series comes to a surprising, breathtaking, and utterly satisfying conclusion. The Garde didn’t start this war, but they’ll do whatever it takes to end it once and for all. . . .<br /> <br />The Mogadorians have invaded Earth. Their warships loom over our most populated cities, and no country will risk taking them head on. The Garde are all that stand in the way, but they’ll need an army of their own to win this fight.<br /> <br />They’ve teamed up with the US military, but it might not be enough. The Garde need reinforcements, and they’ve found them in the most unexpected place. Teenagers from across the globe, like John Smith’s best friend, Sam, have developed abilities. So John and the others must get to them before the Mogs, because if they don’t their enemies will use these gifted teens for their own sinister plan.<br /> <br />But after all the Mogadorians have taken from John—his home, his family, his friends, and the person he loves most—he might not want to put any more lives in danger. He’s got nothing left to lose, and he’s just discovered he has been given an incredible new Legacy. Now he can turn himself into the ultimate weapon. So will he risk his life to save the world, or will he realize that power in numbers will save us all?</span>

Unfortunately, Sarah and mark didn't get any legacies :( .when he gets their he finds that Adam is sitting next to a girl. The girl is number one and she tells them what happened to her. this is actually what happens in the book because i have read it but i am not going to spoil the the ending but i am just saying that Sarah doesn't die. <div id="review_1263901884" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1263901884" />
    <a title="Ricky" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7644190-ricky"><img alt="Ricky" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1544427381p2/7644190.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1263901884?book_show_action=true">Apr 25, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ricky" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ricky" href="/user/show/7644190-ricky">Ricky</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7644190-ricky?shelf=action-adventures">action-adventures</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7644190-ricky?shelf=apocalyptic-or-post-apocalyptic">apocalyptic-or-post-apocalyptic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7644190-ricky?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7644190-ricky?shelf=read-this-if-it-kills-you">read-this-if-it-kills-you</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7644190-ricky?shelf=thrillers">thrillers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7644190-ricky?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7644190-ricky?shelf=freaky-supernatural-adventures">freaky-supernatural-adventures</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7644190-ricky?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7644190-ricky?shelf=why-isn-t-this-a-bloody-movie-yet">why-isn-t-this-a-bloody-movie-yet</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1263901884" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13127719456137317288">It's finally here. <br/><br/>The glorious end of the Lorien Legacies.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417392530ra/12341134.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And holy bloodydamn goryhell, how far this series has come from its beginnings in <i>I Am Number Four.</i> More than any of its predecessors, <i>United As One</i> is dark and intense and unremitting in its pulse-pounding action. It's the <i>Mockingjay</i> or <i>Deathly Hallows</i> of this series, by which point it's all-out war, and everyone's out for blood.<br/><br/>Including our heroes. Including our perennial Boy Scout, John. Now he knows how Marina feels, having lost his</span>
  <span id="freeText13127719456137317288" style="display:none">It's finally here. <br><br>The glorious end of the Lorien Legacies.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417392530ra/12341134.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And holy bloodydamn goryhell, how far this series has come from its beginnings in <i>I Am Number Four.</i> More than any of its predecessors, <i>United As One</i> is dark and intense and unremitting in its pulse-pounding action. It's the <i>Mockingjay</i> or <i>Deathly Hallows</i> of this series, by which point it's all-out war, and everyone's out for blood.<br><br>Including our heroes. Including our perennial Boy Scout, John. Now he knows how Marina feels, having lost his first love forever, and like many of us poor fans, he's not recovered. He's permanently damaged by this, more than any physical battle scar he'll ever get.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441836141ra/16157732.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441836322ra/16157754.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Meanwhile, there are ever more human Garde popping up all over the planet - most of them teenagers, of course. One has to wonder, why teenagers? Because, as some of our favorite Garde come to suspect over the course of this harrowing final novel, perhaps the last of the Loric species won't be enough to stop Setrakus Ra (come on, you didn't think that Satanic piece of shit was really dead at the end of Book 6, did you?)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468710386ra/19739155.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And if the remaining Loric Garde aren't enough, well, that's what the new human Garde are for. They could form the next generation of the resistance if the Loric fail - and that's what really sells this book, because the darkness is so thick that eventually you start to doubt that there'll be a happy ending.<br><br>No spoilers, though.<br><br>If you're like me, you won't be able to put this book down. I read the entire thing in one sitting, it was that amazing. As I said before, this one really ramps the action up to an all-time high, and employs the series' signature move of jumping to the other POV (this one, for the first time since Book 2, contains only two POVs, John and Six) and leaving the previous chapter on a nasty cliffhanger to perhaps its greatest effect since at least <i>The Fall of Five</i>.<br><br>I'm convinced that this book is going to be one of my end-of-year Top 5 winners at the Second Annual Pinecone Awards, certainly beating out such contenders as <i>The Inquisition</i>, <i>Morning Star</i>, <i>Glass Sword</i>, and even <i>Lady Midnight.</i> Perhaps it'll even top the list, although Marie Lu's <i>Midnight Star</i> won't make it easy.<br><br><i>Ave atque vale</i>, Lorien Legacies. And to Hollywood, I say only this - it's a crime that only the first book got a much-deserved (and criminally underrated) movie adaptation. A rebooted movie series is in order, desperately. And may that reboot be every bit as stylish and killer-cool and pitch-perfect as, say, <i>The Amazing Spider-Man</i> or the Marvel Cinematic Universe.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13127719456137317288" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <blockquote>“I am not fucking extinct,” growls Nine.</blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469888008i/19868610._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seven years that I've been into this series, it gives me something that I couldn't figure out until now. Yet every character is a part of my life and I don't want to let it go, no matter what. Nine is always my boy. And I want to see smile on John's face for one last time.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469887279i/19868517.jpg" width="400" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anyway, when I picked this book up, I didn't expected to meet its unexciting ending and I had no idea about the excruciatingly pace either.   <span id="freeText5877746145861953123" style="display:none">I think this is not the last time we're going to read a book about the Garde.<br />I swear Pittacus Lore is brewing something...<br /><br />Annnnd to end it like that?<br /><br />Those bottles of black oils...<br />Then John giving the human Garde the chimaeras...<br /><br /><br />Or its just me making excuses. Just go with the flow.<br /><br />- I actually re-read all the previous Lorien Legacies book before reading UAO. I thought I was preparing myself... Gosh! Maybe after healing him you can just go on your own separate ways... <br />And also, me writing this to you doesn't me I forgive him for mercilessly killing Eight and all of those other things.<br /> <br />-John... of course he's Pittacus Lore! He could freaking heal himself.<br />When Six saw him just lying there... well lets just say that my nose was wet. (Eeew)<br /><br />-Is it bad to feel relieve that Sarah is really dead? I never liked her. I think that sounded so evil.<br /><br />-Mark, his death... it was totally unnecessary.<br /><br />-Dear Pittacus Lore, the author,<br />Are you James Fray?<br /><br /><br />@gleekidMC</span>

<div id="review_1863830405" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1863830405" />
    <a title="Khurram" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25493797-khurram"><img alt="Khurram" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383996638p2/25493797.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1863830405?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Khurram" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Khurram" href="/user/show/25493797-khurram">Khurram</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780718184889" href="/book/show/29776977-united-as-one">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1863830405" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15655657755850997559">Great book. Dark, Intense and Awsome. Every book in this series seem to be improved slightly on the last. I love the character development in the series. There were points in the first couple of book I was thinking to myself about John/4 will you please grow a pair and stop acting like a love sick teenager. Of course this probobly not fair as he actually was a love sick teenager, and had not quite grown into his heroic role as yet. I am actually glad that the books were done this way it made me </span>
  <span id="freeText15655657755850997559" style="display:none">Great book. Dark, Intense and Awsome. Every book in this series seem to be improved slightly on the last. I love the character development in the series. There were points in the first couple of book I was thinking to myself about John/4 will you please grow a pair and stop acting like a love sick teenager. Of course this probobly not fair as he actually was a love sick teenager, and had not quite grown into his heroic role as yet. I am actually glad that the books were done this way it made me appricate the latter book more.<br /><br />In this book the nitration is shared by John/4 and Six. Six has always been the tough warrior compared to Fours more compassionate personality, and she also had an edge in battle as she competent using her powers/legacies. Now John is more battle hardened and with Pittacus Lore's ability to mimic powers/legacies, making not only a one man army, but also possibly the most powerful person on the planet. With possibly the exception of Setrakus Ra. Who is also a genius who has been planning with how to deal with Grades and Legacy wealders for centuries.<br /><br />Another great thing about this book even though Four and Six are definitely the main characters every character has a role to play and no matter how big or small it is it is essential.<br /><br />This is a great finale to the series. I like to think of it as more of an ending to the current story arc, and would love more book on the brave new world the Earth infused with Loric energy has become. Maybe this is wishful thinking on my part but I would love more books. Everything about this book is great, the character development, the action, even the pace is right for every moment of the book. Every time I read a few pagers I wanted to read more.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15655657755850997559" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Ever since The Fate of Ten I was starting to lose interest in this series. I found the writing style to be plain and a majority of the characters to be annoying. I especially did not like the direction this series was going.<br/><br/>This book was not much better than The Fate of Ten. The new characters didn't really play that big of a role.   <span id="freeText15670337544595419859" style="display:none">Mini review:<br /><br />It's not all that surprising that I rated this 2 stars. Ever since The Fate of Ten I was starting to lose interest in this series. I found the writing style to be plain and a majority of the characters to be annoying. I especially did not like the direction this series was going.<br /><br />This book was not much better than The Fate of Ten. The new characters didn't really play that big of a role. They were irrelevant in a way. The pace was really off. And the ending was anticlimactic. By the end of this book some of the characters are happy and are living awesome lives and the other characters futures left a bitter taste in my mouth.<br /><br />The only characters that I liked were Nine, Six, Walker, Sam, and Adam. I really did not like Seven and John. Mark was rather annoying in this book. I felt indifferent to Five and Ella. <br /><br />There were some parts that I enjoyed. It was interesting to see the ending and how everything changed. And how far some of the characters have come. <br /><br />I don't recommend this series. </span>

<div id="review_1901387283" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1901387283" />
    <a title="Kaya" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15462098-kaya"><img alt="Kaya" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1485382914p2/15462098.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1901387283?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kaya" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kaya" href="/user/show/15462098-kaya">Kaya</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1901387283" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3304825504748274851">Words can’t describe how happy I am that this ride is finally over. The series hits rock bottom and I’m not sad to watch it go away. Lorien Legacies had potential, but the writer’s lack of skill and imagination ruined it all. The final book is usually the one with the most action and excitement, but we got neither. <br/><br/>The story dragged in the first half - nothing happens besides the usual stuff - Setrakus Ra goes into hiding and John learns to master his new power. Garde plan their counter strike a</span>
  <span id="freeText3304825504748274851" style="display:none">Words can’t describe how happy I am that this ride is finally over. The series hits rock bottom and I’m not sad to watch it go away. Lorien Legacies had potential, but the writer’s lack of skill and imagination ruined it all. The final book is usually the one with the most action and excitement, but we got neither. <br /><br />The story dragged in the first half - nothing happens besides the usual stuff - Setrakus Ra goes into hiding and John learns to master his new power. Garde plan their counter strike and try to steal the ships. Basically, it’s the recycled plot of the last few books. John should’ve died. Five should’ve stayed dead. There are too many inconsistencies. How can Lorien teenagers tear through Mogs like it’s a piece of cake when adult warriors failed miserably which caused a whole PLANET to be forever unsurvivable? <br /><br />The author finally realized he can't stretch this any longer. This is the last book, and instead of preparing for the final battle, they keep bulshitting each other, because obviously, they had nothing better to do with their time. The plot is identical to the previous volumes - long and predictable. There is an attempt at the bittersweet ending, but I felt like I’m about to get diabetes. The ending is unexciting, the writing style is plain and boring. The final battle was too easily won and anticlimactic when we consider having a build up of six books to reach that goal. From the book 4, this series only went downwards. In book 5 I lost my patience, even though the book had some bright moments. Book 6 was the lowest point and I realized I only feel anger and deep boredom. This novel wasn't much better than the previous one. The pacing was off. The apocalypse that was expected from book 1 never came. Just a long and depressing wrap up of the series. This has been a hard series to get through simply because it's seven books that really could’ve been three or four. <br /><br />All the characters are annoying. The new characters didn't play any role and were a complete waste of paper. I had no idea why the human Garde were introduced if they literally had no purpose. By the end, some characters are happy and live up to their potential, while others’ futures are foggy. All of the important characters survived which is completely unrealistic. <br /><br /><i>I</i> guess I semi-liked Nine, Six and Adam because they were the only rational people who had the guts to do what had to be done. Despite it, they were still stereotypical and didn’t evolve one bit from the first time they appeared. The last book didn't connect the reader to the characters and there was nothing to deepen the story nor relationships. It was basically a marathon to finally see whether or not they will defeat the Mogs and if anyone will die. Half of the characters simply follows John as he saves the day. <br /><br />Moreover, the author learned nothing from the previous volumes since he repeats his old mistakes over and over again. I still didn’t know who's POV the story has been told from, and I’m so done with it, that I don’t even bother to be upset. Numerous times I began reading a chapter with Four visualized in my head, only to realize a few pages later that I should’ve been picturing Six all along. By the way, why is Sam still there? <br /><br />I much preferred this harsher version of John than the whiny brat he's been in the previous books. He almost reminded me of the good lad I really liked in book 1. It seems that finally he found a maturing path, but it’s still quite obvious he doesn’t have what it takes to be an effective leader. Until the day I die, I will be persistent in my belief that John is one of the worst protagonist and heroes ever. <br /><br />Six and Nine went from being two most interesting characters in the earlier books to be Four's cheering squad. I don’t know if it was author’s intention to completely ruin Six’s personality in order for her to become boring like the others, but I’m completely amazed how female voice sounds identical as male.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3304825504748274851" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1572162694" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1572162694" />
    <a title="✨    jamieson   ✨" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7706640-jamieson"><img alt="✨    jamieson   ✨" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499961431p2/7706640.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1572162694?book_show_action=true">Mar 07, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✨    jamieson   ✨" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✨    jamieson   ✨" href="/user/show/7706640-jamieson">✨    jamieson   ✨</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780718184902" href="/book/show/30839584-united-as-one">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=2016-reads">2016-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1572162694" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7630862487892268137"> <b>"I'm not fucking extinct" </b> <br/> - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - -<br/><br/>I've had to say goodbye to a heap of series this year. I mean, so many things are ending in 2016, and the one thats making me the saddest to see go is this goddamn alien book. But I love it so much, and it's been with me for so long. And I can't believe it's over. I can't believe I have to say goodbye to John and Six and Nine and Five and Adam and Marina and Sam and Malcolm and Lexa and BERNIE KOSAR. I'll miss them all s</span>
  <span id="freeText7630862487892268137" style="display:none"> <b>"I'm not fucking extinct" </b> <br /> - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - -<br /><br />I've had to say goodbye to a heap of series this year. I mean, so many things are ending in 2016, and the one thats making me the saddest to see go is this goddamn alien book. But I love it so much, and it's been with me for so long. And I can't believe it's over. I can't believe I have to say goodbye to John and Six and Nine and Five and Adam and Marina and Sam and Malcolm and Lexa and BERNIE KOSAR. I'll miss them all so much, this series is so good. (I literally don't care what any review says this series is SO GOOD) <br /><br />This book picks up a bit after the ending of the Fate of Ten. The gang is quickly reunited and begin to plan their big attack on Setrakus Ra ( bc, duh, that asshole didn't go down aT ALL after FOT) <br /><br />Immediately this book was action packed. This thing is <i>action, action, action </i>the whole way through. It had some INCREDIBLE scenes of mayhem and destruction and <i>SUPERPOWERS</i> that made my trash heart sing. This book is like superpower porn ( my fav kind of porn) <br /><br />Some of the action scenes were ... so good. I mean, I'm used to high quality action scenes - this series has given me so, so many. And still they've managed to be topped off here. <br /><br /><b>I MEAN HECK ! THESE SCENES HAD ME REELING</b> <br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br /><br /> <b>- John's big attack on the Mogs? a m a z i n g. </b> I was SCREAMING @ old Johhny Boy like <br /> omg the way he just went out there and totally wrecked the Mogs I was !!!!!!! kid ur in too <br /> deep and scaring me but also omg you're so incredible <br /> <b>- Throwdown between Five and John ? *fans self* </b> THAT SCENE WAS SO GOOD ! and it <br /> actually got me for 1 hot minute I was a bit confused about Five's intentions and !! I cannot <br /> believe but it was the fight, the throwdown we all had to see and it was so goof <br /> <b> - THE PHIRI DUN RA AND FIVE FIGHT OH MY GOD </b> WHEN FIVE CAME OUT 2 SMAHS HER <br /> I WAS !!!! my son MY SON it was so cool so so cool <br /><b> - Basically the whole scene with the Mog's in West Virginia, actually </b><br /> <b> - THE FINAL SHOWDOWN WITH PHIRI AND ADAM AND SIX </b> SO COOL. I loved to see <br /> Adam fight, loved to see Six fight. Both of them got rekt and I WAS IN DISTRESS but it was a <br /> really nice scene <br /> <b>- THE !!!!!!! SETRAKUS FIGHT. !!</b> it was everything. I was waiting for this fight for 7 books, <br /> the final showdown, the Harry vs Voldermort of the series and boy ! so good. I was a little :/ <br /> about it because I was ?? heck, Johns ximic makes this too easy but OH NO it wasn't easy at <br /> all. I REALLY THOUGHT FIVE WAS A GONER and when Nine lost his arm I WAS YELLING Nine <br /> is my fav so that was NOT a good time for me. But omg !?! that their healing killed him SO <br /> UNEXPECTED. That Marina worked it out ! ? blessing. And omg the fact six did the final dirty <br /> deed SO BEAUTIFUL so poetic I loved it I LOVED IT. <br /> <b> - Six .. when ... sh .. e .... saw John after the fight /cries/. </b> I thought he was dead and I <br /> was like no no no no THIS IS BECOMING ALLEGIANT I didn't like it. So glad he didn't die. I <br /> love John honestly "he's so boring" blah blah idec your fav could never compare<br /><br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />okay. Had to get some emotions out. We're back online with the coherent review.<br /><br />I loved that this book included so many of the scenes that make a final book feel <i>right</i> I mean, there are just some cliches I love to see in a final book and I got a fair few of them in United as One and I loved it. <br /><br />I loved the comparison scenes, with the Garde recognising their power now versus what they were like then. I loved the comparisons made between the Human Garde now and what the Loric were like when they first started developing legacies. I loved the scene when John muses about how 1 piken nearly killed him and Six in Ohio, and how coming up against 3 alone now doesn't even faze him. <br />I'm such a sucker for the "chosen one" trope and the "I was weak, but now I'm strong" trope so honestly this book gave me everything my trash trope loving heard desired. <br /><br />I had some issues with the end, admittedly. Actually, issues isn't the word. The ending wasn't bad, it was fine. But I wish it was MORE. I was disappointed there wasn't more emotional payback in the epilogue. I feel like it's been set up for a possible sequel later, which I'd be on board with. I just wish there'd been MORE from each character, especially Six and Sam. I don't know, it was a weird way to have to say goodbye to them all. <br /><br />But overall I loved this book so much. When I begam reading this I never realised how much it'd grow on me. I DONT EVEN CARE ABOUT ALIENS. BUt I care about <b>these</b> aliens. I'm so glad my fave <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[NINE MY SON <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> made it through. I'm gonna miss this series so much ! I loved these books, loved the characters, loved the romances, loved the action scenes, loved the development of the characters, loved the fights, loved the worldbuilding, loved the banter and the quips. <br /><br />I love it so much, LORIC ARE MY FAVOURITE ALIENS. Thanks @ the world for giving me this #bless. So sad to see them all go. <br /><br /><b>ACTUAL RATING 4.5 !</b><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1685176374" />
    <a title="Ashley Daviau" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35915119-ashley-daviau"><img alt="Ashley Daviau" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1599784716p2/35915119.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1685176374?book_show_action=true">Jun 25, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ashley Daviau" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ashley Daviau" href="/user/show/35915119-ashley-daviau">Ashley Daviau</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1685176374" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11732485409112784639">This book definitely ended the series with the bang I was hoping for! The rest of the series was so action packed and for this book, it felt like all that action was jam packed together for one hell of a finale! <br/><br/>I think my favourite part of this book was seeing how far this series has come since the beginning! This final book takes a much darker turn, so much so that it makes you doubt that any of the characters will get a happy ending other than Setrakus Ra. It's intense and gritty and I loved </span>
  <span id="freeText11732485409112784639" style="display:none">This book definitely ended the series with the bang I was hoping for! The rest of the series was so action packed and for this book, it felt like all that action was jam packed together for one hell of a finale! <br /><br />I think my favourite part of this book was seeing how far this series has come since the beginning! This final book takes a much darker turn, so much so that it makes you doubt that any of the characters will get a happy ending other than Setrakus Ra. It's intense and gritty and I loved every single second of it! <br /><br />There's also some devastating losses that deeply affect our main characters and drastically change them. Mainly John aka Four, he's become permanently damaged and becomes willing to do anything it takes to win the war, no matter the cost and it's almost sad to see him suffer so much! <br /><br />And then we get to the absolutely perfect and stunning ending! I'm not going to lie I definitely shed a few tears, both happy and sad! I've become so invested in this series and these characters after 7 books and it was definitely bittersweet to have it all come to an end. </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_1399403056" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1399403056" />
    <a title="Nadine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3759963-nadine"><img alt="Nadine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1566849081p2/3759963.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1399403056?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nadine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nadine" href="/user/show/3759963-nadine">Nadine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1399403056" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8387301043200877947">WHAT AN EPIC CONCLUSION!!!! I CAN'T EVEN RIGHT NOW.<br/>_____________<br/><br/><br/>I’m going to begin with a mini review of United as One, the conclusion to the series, then review the series as a whole. <b>Scroll down for a spoiler free review of the entire series.</b><br/><br/>United as One has the unfortunate task of concluding this epic series. It has to wrap up all the story lines and give readers the satisfying ending they’ve been pinning for for years. I think it does all that and more. United as One picks up after the even</span>
  <span id="freeText8387301043200877947" style="display:none">WHAT AN EPIC CONCLUSION!!!! I CAN'T EVEN RIGHT NOW.<br />_____________<br /><br /><br />I’m going to begin with a mini review of United as One, the conclusion to the series, then review the series as a whole. <b>Scroll down for a spoiler free review of the entire series.</b><br /><br />United as One has the unfortunate task of concluding this epic series. It has to wrap up all the story lines and give readers the satisfying ending they’ve been pinning for for years. I think it does all that and more. United as One picks up after the events of the previous book, John dealing with Sarah’s death. He’s broken and feels lost, but decides to channel his aggression and frustration into ending Setrákus Ra. As expected, this book focuses heavily on John. Most of the chapters are told from his perspective, but Six and Marina’s chapters are also featured. John is no longer the same character he was in the previous book. He’s a certified badass willing to anything and everything to defeat his enemy. His chapters scared me at some points because I feared for his survival.<br /><br />The ending was explosive and epic. I thoroughly enjoyed every moment of the ultimate conclusion. It kept me on the edge of my seat reading until the last page. I felt like the ending could have used one more chapter, but that didn’t take away from my overall enjoyment. <br /><br />Overall, I’m pleased to say United as One is an epic conclusion to this series and well worth the wait. I thought it was action packed while still being able to slow down the pace without it feeling boring.<br /><br /><br /><br /><b>SPOILER FREE REVIEW OF THE LORiEN LEGACIES…. 4.5 STARS.</b><br /><br />The Lorien Legacies is the epic story about a race of teenage aliens hidden on earth. Each of these teenagers have special abilities that will help them in the future to defeat a looming threat. <br /><br />The first book, I am Number Four, is definitely the weakest book of the series (and don’t get me started on the movie). The reader is introduced to number Four, John, and watches him struggle with wanting to be a normal teenager and the looming threat that dictates his life. This book feels very much like a typical Young Adult book with the ever-present looming threat with a romance thrown in the mix. The real meat of the story doesn’t fully emerge until the second and third books, The Power of Six and The Rise of Nine. Because of this slow start to the story, I know a lot of readers stopped reading so I would encourage those who stopped to finish the series. It is well worth your time.<br /><br />The character in the series are interesting and made me want to know more about their back stories with each book. However, with so many characters in play only the main characters are fully fleshed out. John and Sam are the characters who undergo the most character development. The characters they are at the beginning of the story are not the ones at the ending.<br />I wanted to include Six in the characters who are fully fleshed out, but the more I thought about her the more I realized she didn’t undergo any massive changes. She’s still very much the same generic badass female at the end of the story that she was when she was first introduced.<br />Without going into spoilers, the other characters are given enough depth for the reader to care about them but little else.<br /><br />The action in this series is second to none. It’s chaotic and confusing, but easy to follow. It’s action that keeps you on the edge of your seat because the reader is able to follow each moment with clarity and the reason for this clarity is the writing style. Pittacus Lore’s writing is precise and clear in its meaning. It’s not overly poetic or flowery because it’s direct. Lore understands his audience and caters to them.<br /><br /><br />Overall, The Lorien Legacies is an absolutely amazing and action packed series that will please just about any reader. If you’re looking for an easy quick read that’s jam packed with exciting and intense moments, look no further because this series will blow your socks off!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8387301043200877947" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1710016448" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1710016448" />
    <a title="Ryan Buckby" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32429909-ryan-buckby"><img alt="Ryan Buckby" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528436487p2/32429909.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1710016448?book_show_action=true">Jul 26, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ryan Buckby" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ryan Buckby" href="/user/show/32429909-ryan-buckby">Ryan Buckby</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1710016448" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5460906367085700158"><b> the grade didn't start this war, but they'll do whatever it takes to end it once and for all.. </b><br/><br/>I'M SOOO SAD, its over, the series has come to an end and i'm sad crying almost i don't know how to feel right now there are so many emotions i have but i can't pin point which ones are worse.<br/><br/>This had one of the best series finales i have ever read and i will continue to praise this series over and over, from start to finish i was taken on this crazy journey and it didn't stop until the very end of th</span>
  <span id="freeText5460906367085700158" style="display:none"><b> the grade didn't start this war, but they'll do whatever it takes to end it once and for all.. </b><br /><br />I'M SOOO SAD, its over, the series has come to an end and i'm sad crying almost i don't know how to feel right now there are so many emotions i have but i can't pin point which ones are worse.<br /><br />This had one of the best series finales i have ever read and i will continue to praise this series over and over, from start to finish i was taken on this crazy journey and it didn't stop until the very end of the series. I will forever recommend this series to anyone who needs another series to read because this series is amazing!. i have so many feelings and emotions after finishing this series and the ending was perfect which is hard to do with long running series but this one was just a perfect way to end the series. <br /><br /><b>Plot:</b> the plot continued straight from the sixth book and continued strong throughout the seventh book, i love how this series has stayed strong and consistent throughout seven books and remained strong is difficult to do with long running series. Everything was tied up and resolved in the last book all the information and events that have happened in the passed six books was resolved in one form or another. I feel like there could be another whole new series with a new set of characters because the last book has given that option for there to be another series. I was surprised to learn the humans who got the legacy powers kept them at the end of the war, I honestly thought they would have been taken away but that opens up more options for another series. <br /><br /><b>Characters:</b>my love for these characters is strong and has remained strong throughout the whole series. Marina and Six are two of my favourite characters and there friendship is so strong throughout this book it warms my heart. Theres a conversation in the book between Six and Marina that made me tear up a little <i>
  <b>you've been there for me in the worst times six. You always made me laugh or propped me up, sometimes you literally carried me. I just wanted to tell you that you're pretty much my best friend</b>
</i> I HAVE NEVER FELT MORE HAPPY AND CLOSE TO CRYING IN THAT MOMENT OF A BOOK EVER. John totally did a Marina in this book went a little crazy and had that 'i need to do this' vibe about him during the book, i was worried that he would be pushed over the edge after Sarah's death but i'm so glad the character didn't go that far. Mark died in this book i was glad the character did a complete 180 from the first book and got that story arc that i was hoping he would and i ended up being sad of his death. Sam and Six are finally together it finally happened even though it wasn't seen on the page it was implied that they did especially in the 'One Year Later' events. <br /><br /><b>Setting:</b> this book had so many different settings throughout the whole series of different countries and there were a few that were visited, i have no complaints about it <br /><br />I'm sad this series is over, i really want another series maybe with a new set of characters? maybe some of the humans with legacy powers? so many possibilities! </span>
  <a data-text-id="5460906367085700158" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1450467429" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1450467429" />
    <a title="Niamh" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/49346342-niamh"><img alt="Niamh" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448337650p2/49346342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1450467429?book_show_action=true">Oct 26, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Niamh" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Niamh" href="/user/show/49346342-niamh">Niamh</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780718184902" href="/book/show/30839584-united-as-one">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49346342-niamh?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49346342-niamh?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49346342-niamh?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49346342-niamh?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1450467429" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17126176190846694055"><blockquote>
  <i>"Sydney gets it the worst. ... Images of the opera house in flames, the bridge behind it collapsing..."</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Finally, a U.S.-centric sci-fi/alien invasion book that acknowledges the existence of Australia and the likelihood that at least Sydney will be attacked! But I'm a little biased, so let's move on.<br/><br/>Sometimes with series, the quality of the books declines as the series progresses. I am very pleased to say that, in my opinion, this is not the case here. The authors kept with their usual style, </span>
  <span id="freeText17126176190846694055" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>"Sydney gets it the worst. ... Images of the opera house in flames, the bridge behind it collapsing..."</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Finally, a U.S.-centric sci-fi/alien invasion book that acknowledges the existence of Australia and the likelihood that at least Sydney will be attacked! But I'm a little biased, so let's move on.<br /><br />Sometimes with series, the quality of the books declines as the series progresses. I am very pleased to say that, in my opinion, this is not the case here. The authors kept with their usual style, which has worked so well before, so why change it? The book is action-packed, the perspective changes with each chapter so you are kept on your toes, and often the chapter ends on a mini cliffhanger, so you are left wondering what happened to some characters while reading about what happens to others.<br /><br />I found its representation of war quite realistic. Stuff happens that you can't control, and it would be quite unrealistic for everyone to survive unscathed. And of course everyone will have different reactions to said events, which was well shown.<br /><br />All in all, I really enjoyed reading this book (I finished it way too late for how tired I was feeling), and felt that it ended the series well. Thank you to the authors for letting me have this literary over the past six years.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17126176190846694055" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('2GrfQ77aYbeKzzJawhmen6TGolMWc1uj7qMa30YY+JNlJYtzTDg/hhaSXIprlH6bHCht7gBt99ix1cVaczsZSw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NMff2vbpUs69zmOtYWKhDVJWk1b3HNnCM8HwTCSh8ZyJiIvqBAsM/yGTDX3I70EJ6rhc6+ECdblsty/JEYIQRA==')})
  }
